$Z=j\left( \omega L-\frac{1}{\omega c} \right)$
$\omega_{r}L=\frac{1}{\omega_{r}C}$
$\omega_{r}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}$


capacitor energy$\frac{cur^{2}}{2}$

coil energy $\frac{Lir^{2}}{2}$
Quality factor $Q=\frac{1}{R}\sqrt{ \frac{L}{C} }$

Good quality factor is at least 10

---

ex.1 
$|U|=1$,$R=10Ω$,$L=1H$,$C=1µF$
$\omega_{r}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}=10^{3} \frac{nd}{s}$
$|I_{r}|=\frac{|U|}{R}=0.1A$
$Q=\frac{|V_{cv}|}{|U|}=\frac{|I_{r}|·\omega_{r}L}{|U|}=100$

max voltage = 100V

# Paraller resonance
$Z=\frac{j\omega L\left( \frac{1}{j\omega C} \right)}{j\left( \omega L-\frac{1}{\omega C} \right)}$=$\frac{\frac{L}{C}}{j\left( \omega L-\frac{1}{\omega C} \right)}$=$-j \frac{\frac{L}{C}}{\left( \omega L-\frac{1}{\omega C} \right)}$

$\omega L=\frac{1}{\omega_{r}C}$
$\omega_{r}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}$ - Open circuit

---

Calculate the coil rms voltage at the resonant frequency $\omega=\omega_{r}$: C=10µF, R=40Ω, $e=2\sqrt{ 2 }\sin\omega t \ V$. What is the value in V.

$\omega_{r}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}=10^{3} \frac{rad}{s}$
$I_{r}=\frac{2}{40}=0.05A$

coil
$X_{L}=\omega_{r}L=100Ω$

---

$\omega_{L}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ L_{1}+C_{2} }}$
$\omega_{g}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ L_{e}C_{e} }}$
equivalent intuctance and capacitance
$L_{e}=\frac{L_{1}L_{3}}{L_{1}+L_{3}}$
$\omega_{g}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ \frac{L}{2}·C }}=3535 \frac{rad}{s}$ - max energy
# part 2
$2\pi f$
At what radian frequency does the circuit dissipate the minimum energy

$\omega_{L}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ 160·10^{-9} }}=2500 \frac{rad}{s}$-no energy

$|I_{RMS}|=\frac{\frac{12}{\sqrt{ 2 }}}{R}=8.5mA$

$\omega_{r}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{ LC }}=250 \frac{rad}{s}$

$Z=R+j 1000-j \frac{1}{\omega C}=1000+100j-j \frac{1}{0.5·10^{3}·8·10^{-6}}$=
=$1000+j 750$
$|Z|=1250Ω$
$|I_{RMS}|=\frac{\frac{12}{\sqrt{  2}}}{1.25}mA=6.789mA$

$\lim_{ \omega \to \infty }=\frac{\frac{1}{j\omega C_{2}}}{\frac{1}{j\omega C_{1}}+\frac{1}{j\omega C_{2}}}·\frac{j\omega}{j\omega}=\lim_{ \omega \to \infty } \frac{\frac{1}{C_{2}}}{\frac{1}{C_{1}}+\frac{1}{C_{2}}}=\frac{C_{1}}{C_{1}+C_{2}}$

---

For the given RC circuit: C=7µF, R=9kΩ loaded by the $R_{l}=3kΩ$ resistance, find the gain $k(\omega)$ at the cut-off frequency
